<script type="text/javascript" language="JavaScript">
    var renderedLogo=false;

    function haveAd(str)
    {
        return (str && !str.match(/<!-- PRONTONOAD -->/));
    }

    function shouldShowAd(adName)
    {
        return document.getElementById(adName)
            && document.getElementById(adName).contentWindow
            && document.getElementById(adName).contentWindow.document
            && document.getElementById(adName).contentWindow.document.body
            && haveAd(document.getElementById(adName).contentWindow.document.body.innerHTML);
    }

    function checkAndShowLogo(adName)
    {
        if (shouldShowAd(adName))
        {
            document.getElementById(adName).style.display = '';
            renderedLogo = true;
        }
    }

    function checkAndShowAd(adName)
    {
        if (shouldShowAd(adName))
            document.getElementById(adName).style.display = '';
        else {
            setTimeout(function(){
                if(shouldShowAd(adName))
                    document.getElementById(adName).style.display = '';
            },3000);
    }
    }

    function checkAndShowSlidingAd(adName,surroundingDiv)
    {
        if (shouldShowAd(adName) && document.getElementById(surroundingDiv)) {
            $('#'+surroundingDiv).slideDown(1000);
    }
        else {
            setTimeout(function(){
                if (shouldShowAd(adName) && document.getElementById(surroundingDiv)) {
                        $('#'+surroundingDiv).slideDown(1000);
                    }
                },3000);
            }
        }










    if (renderedLogo)
        document.getElementById('featured_logos').style.display = '';
</script>
